***geschut.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:geschut.html>geschut</a> (8576)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">geschutte</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*gaskutją</i>. <p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:geslacht.html>geslachte</a></i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:slachten.html>slachte</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">slahta</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*slahtō</i>, compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Geschlecht</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">gender, <a href = vnd.unilang:kind.html>kind</a>, lineage</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***geslachtsrijp.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:geslachtsrijp.html>geslachtsrijp</a> (93048)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geslacht.html>geslacht</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-s-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rijp.html>rijp</a></i>, calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">geschlechtsreif</i>. First attested in the 1860s.
</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*gisprekki</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*gasprakją</i>. ***gestaag.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gestaag.html>gestaag</a> (51847)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From earlier <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">gestadig</i> through syncope, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gestadich</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gestedich</i>. Prefixed from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ge-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">stadig</i>, although the unprefixed form <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> now <a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gestaag.html>gestaag</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gestaag.html>gestager</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">gestaagst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>steady, continuous</li>
<li>gradual</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:gesternte.html>gesternte</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gesterte</i>, derived from <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">sterne</i>, an alternative form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:sterre.html>sterre</a></i>, for which see Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ster.html>ster</a></i>. <p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gesticht.html>gesticht</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gestichten.html>gestichten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gesticht.html>gestichtje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> psychiatric ward, mental asylum.</li>
